Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 (Apollo 15-17 Command Module) program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Photography was by Ron Burkey, and transcription was performed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

024378,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
024379,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
024380,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Artemis (i.e., Colossus 3),
024381,000005:                                                                                                  ##              build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM)
024382,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for
024383,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo 15-17.
024384,000008:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
024385,000009:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Jim Lawton <jim DOT lawton AT gmail DOT com>
024386,000010:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
024387,000011:                                                                                                  ## Page Scans:  www.ibiblio.org/apollo/ScansForConversion/Artemis072/
024388,000012:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2010-01-26 JL   Started Artemis072 conversion based on Comanche055 
024389,000013:                                                                                                  ##                              module.
024390,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2010-01-31 JL   Finished Artemis072 conversion. Fixed build errors.
024391,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-01 JL   Fixed build errors.
024392,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-02 JL   Fixed page numbers. Removed duplicated code section
024393,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              on page 611.
024394,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-06 JL   Added missing "DEC 18" instruction. Added missing 
024395,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              code on page 618. Added missing line on page 601. 
024396,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              Fixed line 5 on p580, which is overprinted in the 
024397,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              scan. Fixed an EQUALS on p589. Removed spurious 
024398,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              PUSH on p598.
024399,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-13 JL   Fixed errors on pages 563, 589, 604, 619, 629.
024400,000024:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-20 RSB  Un-##'d this header.
024401,000025:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-05 RSB  Proofed comment text by diff'ing vs Comanche 55
024402,000026:                                                                                                  ##                              and corrected errors found, but only through about 
024403,000027:                                                                                                  ##                              p. 571 so far.  Note that while P20 is supposedly an 
024404,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              identical rev in the the two AGC versions, in fact
024405,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              the comments are rather  different, so that portion
024406,000030:                                                                                                  ##                              was proofed by traditional means, and the same is 
024407,000031:                                                                                                  ##                              true of a lesser degree to the  rest of it as well. 
024408,000032:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-06 RSB  Completed comment-text proofing. In the end, half or
024409,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              more of the file was proofed "traditionally", which
024410,000034:                                                                                                  ##                              has proven to be a pretty hit-and-miss process, so
024411,000035:                                                                                                  ##                              I'd judge that it probably needs still more proofing.
024412,000036:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-06 RSB  Re-proofed comment text using octopus/ProoferComments.
024413,000037:                                                                                                  ##                              The print- and/or scan-quality is so poor that it's 
024414,000038:                                                                                                  ##                              tough to feel much confidence in this method, but 
024415,000039:                                                                                                  ##                              combined with the manual proofing already-done, I 
024416,000040:                                                                                                  ##                              feel much more confident of the results now.
024417,000041:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-17 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified by 4-way diff'ing
024418,000042:                                                                                                  ##                              of Colossus 237 & 249, Comanche 55, and Artemis 72.
024419,000043:                                                                                                  ##              2021-05-30 ABS  NOUTINPT -> NDUTINPT
024420,000044:                                                                                                  ##              2021-10-06 RSB  RANGER0 -> RANGERD

024423,000047: 
024424,000048:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
024425,000049:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
024426,000050:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -1
024427,000051:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
024428,000052: 
024429,000053:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024430,000054: 
024431,000055:                                                                                                  #  TO INITIALIZE THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION SUBROUTINES R22, R61CSM, AND
024432,000056:                                                                                                  #  R52, WHICH IN TURN CONTROL THE CSM ATTITUDE AND OPTICS POSITIONING,
024433,000057:                                                                                                  #  PROCESS BOTH OPTICS AND VHF TRACKING DATA, AND UPDATE EITHER THE LM
024434,000058:                                                                                                  #  OR THE CSM STATE VECTORS.
024435,000059: 
024436,000060:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024437,000061:                                                                                                  #    V37E20E
024438,000062: 
024439,000063:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024440,000064:                                                                                                  #    R22 (RENDEZVOUS TRACK DATA PROCESSING)
024441,000065:                                                                                                  #    R52 (AUTO OPTICS POSITIONING)
024442,000066:                                                                                                  #    R61CSM (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
024443,000067:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH            BANKCALL            UPFLAG
024444,000068:                                                                                                  #    DOWNFLAG           2PHSCHNG            LOADTIME
024445,000069:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           UPSTATE             INTPRET
024446,000070:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           MKRLEES             FINDVAC
024447,000071: 
024448,000072:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
024449,000073:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
024450,000074:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
024451,000075: 
024452,000076:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES
024453,000077:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024454,000078: 
024455,000079:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024456,000080:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024457,000081: 
024458,000082:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
024459,000083:                                                                                                  #    RNDVZFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG, TARG1FLG
024460,000084:                                                                                                  #    PRFTRKAT, V50N18FL
024461,000085: 
024462,000086: 36,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S7                                 
024463,000087: 36,2000                                           BANK                                           
024464,000088: 
024465,000089: 36,2016  E6,1774                                  EBANK=   R61CNTR                               
024466,000090: 36,2016                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
024467,000091: 
024468,000092: 36,2016           04636        PROG20             TC       BANKCALL                              
024469,000093: 36,2017           03731                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
024470,000094:                                                                                                  #  BLOCKING OF UPLINK IS DONE BY UPLINK PRG
024471,000095: 36,2020           31655                           CA       ADB                                   
024472,000096: 36,2021           55773                           TS       DBPTC

025102,000726:                                                                                                  #    THE SXT TRUNNION ANGLE AND TO STORE THE MEASURED TRUNNION BIAS FOR P23

025192,000816: 
025193,000817:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R21)
025194,000818:                                                                                                  #  AND BACKUP SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R23)
025195,000819: 
025196,000820:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
025197,000821:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 1
025198,000822:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
025199,000823:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025200,000824: 
025201,000825:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM SIGHTING MARKS IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIG-
025202,000826:                                                                                                  #  ATION PROGRAM. CALLED BY ASTRONAUT VIA EXTENDED VERB
025203,000827:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
025204,000828:                                                                                                  #          R21 VIA V 57
025205,000829:                                                                                                  #          R23 VIA V 54
025206,000830:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
025207,000831:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
025208,000832:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      GOMARK2         GOMARKF
025209,000833:                                                                                                  #    INTPRET       GENTRAN         KLEENEX
025210,000834:                                                                                                  #    ENDMARK
025211,000835:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
025212,000836:                                                                                                  #    MARKRUPT USED BY SXTMARK HAS BEEN MODIFIED TO STORE MARK IN MRKBUF2
025213,000837:                                                                                                  #  FOR USE BY R22. WHEN ASTRONAUT IS FINISHED TAKING MARKS, HE HITS AN
025214,000838:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED ,   R21 IS TERMINATED THUS CAUSING THE FINAL MARK TO BE TRANSFRD
025215,000839:                                                                                                  #  TO MRKBUF2 FOR PROCESSING BY R22
025216,000840:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
025217,000841:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025218,000842:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
025219,000843:                                                                                                  #    7 REGISTER MRKBUF2 CONTAINING TIME2,TIME1,CDUY,OPTICS X,CDUZ, OPTICS Y,
025220,000844:                                                                                                  #  CDUX.
025221,000845:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025222,000846:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET AND RESET
025223,000847:                                                                                                  #    R21MARK   (COMMUNICATION TO MARKRUPT TO STORE MARKS IN MRKBUF1 + 2)
025224,000848:                                                                                                  #    R23FLG  INDICATES COAS MARKING
025225,000849:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025226,000850: 37,2263  E7,1722                                  EBANK=   MRKBUF1                               
025227,000851: 37,2000                                           SETLOC   RENDEZ                                
025228,000852: 37,2000                                           BANK

025382,001006: 
025383,001007:                                                                                                  #   BVECTOR PERFORMS COMPUTATIONS FOR
025384,001008:                                                                                                  #  DELTAQ,THE MEASURED DEVIATION BASED ON THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE CSM-LE
025385,001009:                                                                                                  #  M STATE VECTOR ESTIMATES AND THE ACTUAL TRACKING MEASUREMENT.
025386,001010:                                                                                                  #  US,THE MODIFIED FICTITIOUS STAR DIRECTION VECTOR
025387,001011:                                                                                                  #  GEOMETRY VECTOR B ASSOCIATED WITH EACH TRACKING MEASUREMENT.
025388,001012:                                                                                                  #  INPUT
025389,001013:                                                                                                  #     UM,1/2 UNIT VECTOR ALONG THE CSM-LM LINE OF SIGHT (BASIC REF.SYSTEM)
025390,001014:                                                                                                  #     USTAR,FICTITIOUS STAR DIRECTION (1/2 UNIT VECTOR)
025391,001015:                                                                                                  #     RCLP,RELATIVE CSM TO LM POSITION VECTOR
025392,001016:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025393,001017:                                                                                                  #     USTAR,MODIFIED FICTITOUS STAR DIRECTION (1/2 UNIT VECTOR)
025394,001018:                                                                                                  #     BVECTOR = 9 DIMENSIONAL BVECTOR (1/2 UNIT VEC.)
025395,001019:                                                                                                  #     DELTAQ = MEASURED DEVIATION
025396,001020:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025397,001021:                                                                                                  #     L  CALL BVECTORS
025398,001022:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT
025399,001023:                                                                                                  #     L+1 OF CALLING SEQUENCE

025467,001091: 
025468,001092:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING DATA PROCESSING ROUTINE (R22)
025469,001093: 
025470,001094:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025471,001095: 
025472,001096:                                                                                                  #  TO PROCESS RENDEZVOUS SIGHTING MARK AND VHF RANGING DATA TO UPDATE 
025473,001097:                                                                                                  #  THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER THE CSM OR LM AS DEFINED BY VEHUPFLG.
025474,001098:                                                                                                  #  (VEHUPFLG IS SET TO LM BY P20, CSM BY V81E, AND LM BY V80E.)
025475,001099: 
025476,001100:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025477,001101:                                                                                                  #    AUTOMATICALLY SELECTED BY P20
025478,001102: 
025479,001103:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025480,001104:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           INTPRET             GRP2PC
025481,001105:                                                                                                  #    GETUM              BVECTORS            INCORP1
025482,001106:                                                                                                  #    INCORP2            INTEGRV             PHASCHNG
025483,001107:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC              BANKCALL            GOTOV56
025484,001108:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           INSTALL             DOWNFLAG
025485,001109:                                                                                                  #    TRFAILOF           TRFAILON            TASKOVER
025486,001110:                                                                                                  #    POSTJUMP
025487,001111: 
025488,001112:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
025489,001113:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
025490,001114:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
025491,001115: 
025492,001116:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS OR ABORT EXIT MODES
025493,001117:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025494,001118: 
025495,001119:                                                                                                  #  INPUT
025496,001120:                                                                                                  #    MARK DATA, SEE R21 AND R23
025497,001121:                                                                                                  #    VHF RANGING DATA
025498,001122: 
025499,001123:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025500,001124:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT, NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025501,001125:                                                                                                  #    VHFCNT, NO OF VHF RANGING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025502,001126:                                                                                                  #    V06N49, EXCESSIVE UPDATE PARAMETERS-DELTA R AND DELTA V
025503,001127: 
025504,001128:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
025505,001129:                                                                                                  #    SOURCFLG, VINTFLAG, DIM0FLAG, INCORFLG, ORBWFLAG, RENDWFLG
025506,001130:                                                                                                  #    STATEFLG, D6OR9FLG, SKIPVHF, DMENFLG                                 AT THE INTERRUPTED DISPLAY.
025507,001131: 
025508,001132: 34,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S3

026236,001860: 04,3300           52005                           DTCF                                           
026237,001861: 
026238,001862: 04,3301           00440        90MSCALR           OCT      440                                   #  90 MILLISEC IN SCALAR
026239,001863: 04,3302           77754        -DTSCALR           OCT      77754                                 #  -5.9375 MS IN SCALAR
026240,001864: 
026241,001865:                                                                                                  #  CRS61.1       4/10/68
026242,001866:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES

Page 593 

026244,001868:                                                                                                  #  OPTICS TRACKING OF THE LM AND LM TRACKING OF THE CSM RADAR TRANSPONDER
026245,001869:                                                                                                  #  AND TO COMPUTE THE &X-AXIS TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES
026246,001870:                                                                                                  #  COAS TRACKING OF THE LM.
026247,001871:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE SELECTED TRACKING ATTITUDE IF THE 
026248,001872:                                                                                                  #  MANEUVER IS LESS THAN 10 DEGREES BUT TO CALL R60 IF THE MANEUVER IS
026249,001873:                                                                                                  #  GREATER THAN 10 DEGREES OR IF THE R60FLAG IS SET.
026250,001874:                                                                                                  #           (1) EXTRAPOLATE LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS TO PRESENT TIME USING
026251,001875:                                                                                                  #               CONIC EQUATIONS.
026252,001876: 
026253,001877:                                                                                                  #           (2) CALCULATE LOS FROM CSM TO LM = RL - RC.
026254,001878: 
026255,001879:                                                                                                  #           (3) THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE IS DEFINED AS FOLLOWS:
026256,001880:                                                                                                  #               THE TRACK AXIS (I) IS ALIGNED ALONG THE LOS TO THE LM. THE
026257,001881:                                                                                                  #               TRACK AXIS (I) IS DEFINED AS:
026258,001882: 
026259,001883:                                                                                                  #               UNIT(I)=UNIT(Z  )COS55 &UNIT(X  )SIN55
026260,001884:                                                                                                  #                     -       -SC             -SC
026261,001885:                                                                                                  #           (4) COMPUTE DESIRED CDU ANGLES, USING VECPOINT.
026262,001886:                                                                                                  #           (7) FORM DIFFERENCE BETWEEN DESIRED AND ACTUAL CDUS.
026263,001887:                                                                                                  #               IF ANY OF THE THREE ANGLE DIFFERENCES EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES,
026264,001888:                                                                                                  #               GROSS MANEUVER IS REQUIRED. SIGNAL R61 (SET MPAC=1) TO
026265,001889:                                                                                                  #               OPERATE KALCMANU AND EXIT CRS61.1.
026266,001890:                                                                                                  #               IF ALL DIFFERENCES ARE LESS THAN 10 DEGREES, CONTINUE.
026267,001891: 
026268,001892:                                                                                                  #           (8) CALCULATE ORTHOGONAL LOS RATE IN REF COORDS AS
026269,001893: 
026270,001894:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATH = (UNITLOS(B1) X UNITDV(B1))(ABSDV(B7)/ABSLOS(B29))
026271,001895:                                                                                                  #               CONVERSION FACTOR OF 100/2PI (B4) REV CSEC PER RAD SEC IS
026272,001896:                                                                                                  #               APPLIED TO YIELD UNITS OF REVS/SEC. SCALE IS CARRIED AS
026273,001897:                                                                                                  #               B+1+1+7-29+4+1 PLUS RESULTS OF NORMALIZING ABSDV, ABSLOS.
026274,001898:                                                                                                  #               THE EXTRA B+1 RESULTS FROM RESCALING ABSDV B8 AFTER NORM
026275,001899:                                                                                                  #               TO AVOID OVFLOW ON DIVIDE.
026276,001900: 
026277,001901:                                                                                                  #               UNITLOS = UNIT( RL - RC) B1.
026278,001902:                                                                                                  #               UNITDY  = UNIT( VL - VC) B1.
026279,001903:                                                                                                  #               ABSLOS  = LENGTH OF LOS, METERS B29.
026280,001904:                                                                                                  #               ABSDV   = LENGTH OF DV , METERS/CSEC B7.
026281,001905: 
026282,001906:                                                                                                  #           (9) OBTAIN RATE IN SM COORDS.
026283,001907: 
026284,001908:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATHSM = (REFSMMAT)(OMEGATH).
026285,001909: 
026286,001910:                                                                                                  #           (10)OBTAIN GIMBAL ANGLE INCREMENTS FOR 0.1 SECOND.
026287,001911: 
026288,001912:                                                                                                  #               DTHETASM = (0.1)(OMEGATHSM)
026289,001913: 
026290,001914:                                                                                                  #           (11)OBTAIN DELCDUX,Y,Z USING SUBR SMCDURES.
026291,001915:                                                                                                  #               INPUT CONSISTS OF
026292,001916: 
026293,001917:                                                                                                  #               (A) VECTOR OF ANGULAR INCREMENTS, DTHETASM, STORED

Page 594 

026295,001919:                                                                                                  #                   IN V(DTHETASM).
026296,001920: 
026297,001921:                                                                                                  #               (B) SIN,COS CDUX,Y,Z FROM  SUBR CDUTRIG.
026298,001922: 
026299,001923:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OUTPUT OF SMCDURES FROM V(DCDU) TO VAC14D.
026300,001924: 
026301,001925:                                                                                                  #           (12)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN BODY(NB) COORDS USING SUBR SMNB.
026302,001926: 
026303,001927:                                                                                                  #               OMEGANB = (SMNB)(OMEGATHSM)
026304,001928: 
026305,001929:                                                                                                  #               SUBR SMNB REQUIRES  OMEGATHSM IN V(VAC32D) AND ACTUAL CDUS
026306,001930:                                                                                                  #               (Y,X,Z ORDER) IN V(VAC20D) WITH S1 OF VAC = BASE ADDRESS
026307,001931:                                                                                                  #               OF CDUS (FIXLOC + 20D).
026308,001932: 
026309,001933:                                                                                                  #           (13)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN CONTROL COORDS AS FOLLOWS
026310,001934: 
026311,001935:                                                                                                  #               WBODY = (MBDYTCTL)(OMEGANB)   UNITS=REVS/SEC(B0).
026312,001936: 
026313,001937:                                                                                                  #                              ( 0.5       0             0      ) BODY TO
026314,001938:                                                                                                  #               MBDYTCTL(B1) = (  0   COS(7.25)B1  -SIN(7.25)B1 )=CONTROL
026315,001939:                                                                                                  #                              (  0   SIN(7.25)B1   COS(7.25)B1 ) AXES
026316,001940:                                                                                                  #                                                                CONVERSION
026317,001941:                                                                                                  #                                                                 MATRIX
026318,001942: 
026319,001943:                                                                                                  #           (14)RESCALE WBODY TO UNITS OF 450 DEG/SEC BY APPLYING FACTOR
026320,001944:                                                                                                  #               OF 0.8 TO REVS/SEC.
026321,001945: 
026322,001946:                                                                                                  #           (15)ADDRESS LIVE AUTOPILOT REGISTERS IN BASIC (UNDER INHINT).
026323,001947: 
026324,001948:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DESIRED CDUS, SCALED 180 DEGREES, FROM T(SAVEDCDU)
026325,001949:                                                                                                  #               TO V(CDUXD).
026326,001950:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DELCDUS, SCALED 180 DEG, FROM V(VAC14D)
026327,001951:                                                                                                  #               TO V(DELCDUX).
026328,001952:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OMEGA CONTROL, SCALED 450 DEG/SEC, FROM V(MPAC)
026329,001953:                                                                                                  #               TO V(WBODY).
026330,001954:                                                                                                  #               RELINT, SET MPAC=0, EXIT CRS61.1
026331,001955: 
026332,001956:                                                                                                  #  CALL     L  CALL CRS61.1
026333,001957: 
026334,001958:                                                                                                  #  RETURNS  ALL TO L+1.
026335,001959: 
026336,001960:                                                                                                  #           (1) S(MPAC)=0. NORMAL EXIT. 3 SETS OF INPUTS FED TO DAP.
026337,001961:                                                                                                  #           (2) S(MPAC)=1. CALCULATED DESIRED CDUS,SP, SET IN T(CPHI)
026338,001962:                                                                                                  #               FOR KALCMANU. ABS(ACDU - DCDU) EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES.
026339,001963:                                                                                                  #           (3) S(MPAC)=2. GNCS AUTO MODE NOT SELECTED (BIT10=1).
026340,001964:                                                                                                  #           (4) S(MPAC)=3. DAP HOLD FLAG (HOLDFLAG) NOT EQUAL -1.
026341,001965: 
026342,001966:                                                                                                  #  INPUT    (1) TIME2,TIME1. COMPUTER CLOCK TIME,DP, CENTISEC B28.
026343,001967:                                                                                                  #           (2) CDUX,Y,Z. PRESENT CDU ANGLES,SP,2S COMPL HALF-REVS B0.
026344,001968:                                                                                                  #           (3) M(REFSMMAT),STABLE MEMBER COORDS B1.

Page 595 

026346,001970: 
026347,001971:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT   NORMAL. EXIT WITH S(MPAC) = 0.
026348,001972: 
026349,001973:                                                                                                  #           (1) CDUXD,CDUYD,CDUZD, DESIRED OUTER, INNER, MIDDLE CDU ANGLES,
026350,001974:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEGREES (HALF-REVS B0).
026351,001975:                                                                                                  #           (2) DELCDUX,DELCDUY,DELCDUZ. 0.1 SEC DCU ANGULAR INCREMENTS,
026352,001976:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEG.
026353,001977:                                                                                                  #           (3) WBODY,WBODY1,WBODY2. LOS ANGULAR RATE IN CONTROL COORDS,
026354,001978:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 450 DEG/SEC.
026355,001979: 
026356,001980:                                                                                                  #               SPECIAL. EXIT WITH S(MPAC) = 1.
026357,001981: 
026358,001982:                                                                                                  #           (1) CPHI,CTHETA,CPSI. DESIRED OUTER, INNER, MIDDLE CDU ANGLES,
026359,001983:                                                                                                  #               SP, 2S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEGREES.
026360,001984: 
026361,001985:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL SUBROUTINES USED   (B)=BASIC
026362,001986: 
026363,001987:                                                                                                  #           (1) CALCGA    (5) LOADTIME(B)  (9) SMNB
026364,001988:                                                                                                  #           (2) CDUTRIG   (6) MATMOVE
026365,001989:                                                                                                  #           (3) CSMCONIC  (7) RDCDUS(B)
026366,001990:                                                                                                  #           (4) LEMCONIC  (8) SMCDURES
026367,001991: 
026368,001992:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE (1) S(Q611),EBANK7  CRS61.1 EXIT .
026369,001993:                                                                                                  #           (2) S(Q6111)EBANK7  CALCDCDU EXIT.
026370,001994:                                                                                                  #           (3) T(SAVEDCDU) E6  SP VECTOR OF CDUDS.
026371,001995:                                                                                                  #           (4) V(SAVEPOS)  E7  CSM POS VEC AND  D(SAVEPOS)= LENGTH OF LOS.
026372,001996:                                                                                                  #           (5) V(SAVEVEL) E7  CSM VEL VEC.
026373,001997: 
026374,001998:                                                                                                  #  FLAGWDS  HOLDFLAG. USED, NOT SET.
026375,001999: 
026376,002000:                                                                                                  #  MISC     (1) ERASABLE ITEMP1 USED TO TEMP STORE EBANK UNDER INHINT.

Page 609 

027000,002624: 
027001,002625:                                                                                                  #  ..... S22.1 ORBITAL NAVIGATION ROUTINE
027002,002626:                                                                                                  #  MOD 1
027003,002627: 
027004,002628:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
027005,002629:                                                                                                  #   1. UPDATE CSM STATE VECTOR
027006,002630:                                                                                                  #   2. UPDATE LANDMARK POSITION
027007,002631:                                                                                                  #   3. CONVERT W MATRIX FROM 9 TO 6 DIMENSIONS
027008,002632: 
027009,002633:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
027010,002634:                                                                                                  #   INTSTALL,INTEGRV,GETUM,SETRE,R-TO-TP,RP-TO-R,BVECTORS,INCORP1,INCORP2
027011,002635:                                                                                                  #   LALOTORV,S22F2410,LAT-LONG,ROWDOT
027012,002636: 
027013,002637:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION
027014,002638:                                                                                                  #   W=9X9 MATRIX
027015,002639:                                                                                                  #   ORBWFLAG=0 FOR INVALID W MATRIX,=1 FOR VALID W MATRIX
027016,002640:                                                                                                  #   ASTRONAUT ENTRY OF KNOWN,L,OFF
027017,002641:                                                                                                  #   8NN= NUMBER OF MARKS  DECIMAL INTEGER B-14
027018,002642:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT= TRANSFORMATION MATRIX
027019,002643:                                                                                                  #   MARKSTAT= ADDRESS OF START OF MARK DATA (MARK DATA OF EACH MARK IS
027020,002644:                                                                                                  #             STORED AS FOLLOWS,  TIME,AIG,SA,AMG,PA,AOG) TIME IS IN DOUBLE
027021,002645:                                                                                                  #             PRECISION,ALL OTHERS ARE IN SINGLE PRECISION
027022,002646:                                                                                                  #   CSM STATE VECTOR
027023,002647: 
027024,002648:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
027025,002649:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED CSM STATE VECTOR
027026,002650:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED LANDMARK POSITION
027027,002651:                                                                                                  #   NEW 6 DIMENSIONAL W MATRIX
027028,002652: 
027029,002653:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
027030,002654:                                                                                                  #   PUSH LIST,CSMPOS,ALPHAV,ERADM,UM,RCLP,USTAR,VARIANCE,X789,BVECTOR,8KK,
027031,002655:                                                                                                  #   S22LOC,SVMRKDAT TABLE,22SUBSCL,LANDMARK,CXOFF,S22C,LAT,LONG,ALT,
027032,002656:                                                                                                  #   TEMPOR1,S22TOFF,S221OFF,DSPTEM1,S22EORM,S22TPRIM
027033,002657: 
027034,002658: 30,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S6                                 
027035,002659: 30,2000                                           BANK                                           
027036,002660: 
027037,002661: 30,2466  E7,1751                                  EBANK=   LANDMARK

027757,003381: 
027758,003382:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINE NAME:   V89CALL
027759,003383:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO:  0                      DATE: 8 FEB 1968
027760,003384:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY:  DIGITAL DEVEL GROUP    LOG SECTION:  P20-P25
027761,003385: 
027762,003386:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
027763,003387: 
027764,003388:                                                                                                  #  CALLED BY VERB 89 ENTER DURING P00. PRIO 10 USED. CALCULATES AND
027765,003389:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS FINAL GIMBAL ANGLES TO POINT CSM +X AXIS OR PREFERRED AXIS
027766,003390:                                                                                                  #  (UNIT(Z)COS55 DEG + UNIT(X)SIN55 DEG) AT LM.
027767,003391: 
027768,003392:                                                                                                  #  1. KEY IN V 89 E ONLY IF IN PROG 00. IF NOT IN P00, OPERATOR ERROR AND
027769,003393:                                                                                                  #  EXIT R63, OTHERWISE CONTINUE.
027770,003394: 
027771,003395:                                                                                                  #  2. IF IN P00, DO IMU STATUS CHECK (R02BOTH). IF IMU ON AND ITS
027772,003396:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION KNOWN TO CGC, CONTINUE.
027773,003397: 
027774,003398:                                                                                                  #  3. FLASH DISPLAY V 04 N 06. R2 INDICATES WHICH SPACECRAFT AXIS IS TO
027775,003399:                                                                                                  #  BE POINTED AT LM.  INITIAL CHOICE IS PREFERRED AXIS. (R2=1).
027776,003400:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT CAN CHANGE TO (+X) AXIS (R2 NOT= 1) BY V22 E 2 E.  CONTINUE
027777,003401:                                                                                                  #  AFTER KEYING IN PROCEED.
027778,003402: 
027779,003403:                                                                                                  #  4. SET PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG ACCORDING TO OPTION DESIRED. SET FLAG
027780,003404:                                                                                                  #  FOR PREFERRED AXIS. RESET FLAG FOR X AXIS.
027781,003405: 
027782,003406:                                                                                                  #  5. CURRENT TIME IS STORED AND R63COMP IS CALLED
027783,003407: 
027784,003408:                                                                                                  #      R63COMP JOB:
027785,003409:                                                                                                  #        
027786,003410:                                                                                                  #        UPDATES CSM AND LM STATE VECTORS USING CONIC EQUATIONS
027787,003411: 
027788,003412:                                                                                                  #        CALCULATES BOTH PREFERRED AND X AXIS TRACKING ATT FROM 3SM TO LM.
027789,003413: 
027790,003414:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES AS INDICATED BY PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG
027791,003415:                                                                                                  #        ARE STORED FOR LATER R60CSM CALL.
027792,003416: 
027793,003417:                                                                                                  #  6. FLASH DISPLAY V 06 N18 AND AWAIT RESPONSE.
027794,003418: 
027795,003419:                                                                                                  #  7. RECYCLE- RETURN TO STEP 5.
027796,003420:                                                                                                  #     TERMINATE- EXIT R63 ROUTINE
027797,003421:                                                                                                  #     PROCEED- RESET 3AXISFLG AND CALL R60CSM FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
027798,003422: 
027799,003423: 
027800,003424:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: V 89 E
027801,003425: 
027802,003426:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED: CHKPOOH, R02BOTH, GOXDSPF, R63COMP, R60CSM
027803,003427: 
027804,003428:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS   1. OPERATOR ERROR IF NOT IN P00
027805,003429:                                                                                                  #           2. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU IS OFF
027806,003430:                                                                                                  #           3. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU ORIENTATION IS UNKNOWN

Page 626 

027808,003432: 
027809,003433:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: NONE
027810,003434: 
027811,003435:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  OPTION1, OPTION1+1, PRFTRKAT(PREF ATT FLAG),P21TIME, 3AXISFLG
027812,003436: 
027813,003437: 23,3143           00000 13560  DP1MIN             2DEC     6000       B-28

027871,003495:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME- P23 CISLUNAR MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION
027872,003496:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO
027873,003497:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY- TOM KNATT
027874,003498:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION- DO MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION BY INCORPORATION OF STAR 
027875,003499:                                                                                                  #  /EARTH AND STAR/MOON OPTICAL MEASUREMENTS.
027876,003500:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE- ASTRONAUT OPERATED

027885,003509:                                                                                                  #  IF LANDMARK IS USED,        NEAR OR FAR HORIZON IF HORIZON IS USED, AND 
027886,003510:                                                                                                  #  BODY TO BE MARKED ON (EARTH OR MOON).  SEE GSOP CHAPT 4.
